# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Grafana Legacy Alerting to Unified Alerting Migration

## Your Task

Find all Go source files in grafana/grafana that implement both the legacy alerting engine and the unified alerting (ngalert) engine: the legacy alert rule storage, the unified alert rule storage, and the migration script that converts legacy rules to unified format.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the migration domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/grafana--26d36ec.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/grafana--26d36ec` (grafana/grafana)
- `sg-evals/grafana-loki` (grafana/loki)
- `sg-evals/grafana-mimir` (grafana/mimir)

Perfect! I've successfully identified and documented all the Go source files in grafana/grafana that implement both the legacy alerting engine and the unified alerting (ngalert) migration. Here's a summary of what I found:

## Key Findings:

### **Legacy Alerting Storage** (in `alert_mig.go`)
- `alert` table - Dashboard-based alert definitions
- `alert_notification` table - Legacy notification channels
- `alert_notification_journal` table - Notification send history
- `alert_rule_tag` table - Alert tag associations

### **Unified Alerting (ngalert) Storage** (in `ualert/tables.go`)
- `alert_rule` table - Core alert rule definitions
- `alert_rule_version` table - Version history tracking
- `alert_instance` table - Current alert state
- `alert_configuration` table - Alertmanager configurations
- `alert_configuration_history` table - Configuration change history

### **Main Migration Scripts** (in `ualert/` directory)
- **ualert.go** - Main migration logic (`upgradeNgAlerting` struct)
- **org_upgrade_state_mig.go** - Organization migration state tracking
- **migration_service_migration.go** - Migration status management
- Plus 7 additional migration files for versioning, rules, and settings

### **Storage Layer Implementation**
- **alert_rule.go** - Unified alert rule database operations
- **legacy_storage/** - Compatibility layer for alertmanager configs
- **provisioning/** - Alert rule service implementations

### **Migration Infrastructure**
- **Dual-write layer** - Simultaneous writes to legacy and unified storage
- **Worker process** - Orchestrates the migration workflow
- **Storage switcher** - Manages transitions between storage systems

Introduce an Alpha version (`v1alpha1`).\n237: 2. **Implement handlers:** Create Resource API handlers (CRUD) interacting with legacy storage. The goal for the initial alpha version is to expose the current functionality of the legacy API through the new Resource API structure, using CUE for schema def ... [line truncated]\n238: 3. **Add feature flag:** Create a flag (e.g., `kubernetesClient<Resource>`), initially off.\n239: 4. **Implement routing/translation:** Modify Legacy API handlers to check the flag and delegate calls to the Resource API or storage layer when active.\n240: 5. **Testing & promotion (Beta):** Enable the flag by default after testing. Promote API to Beta (`v1beta1`). set of Go source files that handle database schema migrations, storage layer abstractions, and API handlers.\\n\\n## Legacy Alerting Storage\\n\\nThe legacy alerting system stores alert rules and configurations in the following database tables:\\n- `alert` table (pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/alert_mig.go:8-37) - Stores dashboard-based alert definitions with fields like dashboard_id, panel_id, name, message, and state\\n- `alert_notification` table (pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/alert_mig.go:90-104) - Stores legacy notification channels with org_id, name, and type\\n- `alert_notification_journal` table (pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/alert_mig.go:138-150) - Tracks notification send history\\n- `alert_rule_tag` table (pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/alert_mig.go:47-86) - Associates tags with alert rules\\n\\n## Unified Alerting (ngalert) Storage\\n\\nThe unified alerting system implements a new database schema with versioning and state management:\\n- `alert_rule` table (pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/ualert/tables.go:200-307) - Core alert rule definitions with org_id, title, condition, data, namespace_uid, and rule_group\\n- `alert_rule_version` table (pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/ualert/tables.go:311-382) - Maintains version history of alert rules with parent_version, restored_from tracking\\n- `alert_instance` table (pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/ualert/tables.go:142-196) - Tracks current state of alert rule instances\\n- `alert_definition` and `alert_definition_version` tables (pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/ualert/tables.go:59-140) - Early intermediate tables (later dropped)\\n- `alert_configuration` table (pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/ualert/tables.go:384-416) - Stores alertmanager configurations per organization\\n- `alert_configuration_history` table (pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/ualert/tables.go:418-437) - Maintains configuration change history\\n\\n## Main Migration Code\\n\\nThe core migration logic is implemented in:\\n- `pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/ualert/ualert.go` - The `upgradeNgAlerting` and related structs manage the migration from legacy to unified alerting, including handling of alertmanager configuration files and organization-specific settings\\n- `pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/ualert/org_upgrade_state_mig.go` - The `CreateOrgMigratedKVStoreEntries` function tracks migration status per organization, managing transitions between Legacy and UnifiedAlerting states\\n- `pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/ualert/migration_service_migration.go` - The `MigrationServiceMigration` function moves legacy alert migration status from migration log to kvstore\\n\\n## Alert Rule Models and Storage\\n\\nThe unified alerting system defines:\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/models/alert_rule.go` - Contains the `AlertRule` struct with comprehensive fields including labels, annotations, no_data_state, exec_err_state, dashboard_uid, panel_id, and special migration labels (MigratedLabelPrefix, MigratedUseLegacyChannelsLabel)\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/store/alert_rule.go` - Implements `DeleteAlertRulesByUID`, `ListAlertRules`, and other database operations for unified alert rules\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/store/models.go` - Defines the `alertRule` and `alertRuleVersion` ORM models\\n\\n## Legacy Storage Compatibility Layer\\n\\nThe notifier package provides a legacy storage compatibility layer:\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/legacy_storage/persist.go` - Defines the `AMConfigStore` interface for alertmanager configuration storage\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/legacy_storage/config.go` - Implements `NewAlertmanagerConfigStore` for managing legacy alertmanager configurations\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/legacy_storage/receivers.go` - Manages receiver (notification channel) configurations\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/legacy_storage/compat.go` - Contains compatibility functions like `GetReceiverProvenance` for converting legacy receivers to unified format\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/legacy_storage/errors.go` - Defines error types for alertmanager configuration\\n\\n## Provisioning and API Layer\\n\\nThe provisioning system handles alert rule management:\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/provisioning/alert_rules.go` - Implements `AlertRuleService` with methods `CreateAlertRule`, `UpdateAlertRule`, `GetAlertRule` for managing alert rules\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/provisioning/contactpoints.go` - Manages notification endpoints (receivers) in the unified system\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/provisioning/persist.go` - Defines `RuleStore` interface for persistence operations\\n- APIs\\n\\n## Migration Infrastructure\\n\\nThe migration system provides several layers:\\n- `pkg/registry/apis/provisioning/jobs/migrate/worker.go` - The `MigrationWorker` struct orchestrates migration between legacy and unified storage\\n- `pkg/registry/apis/provisioning/jobs/migrate/legacy.go` - Implements `LegacyMigrator` for migrating legacy resources\\n- `pkg/storage/legacysql/dualwrite/types.go` - Defines `StorageStatus` tracking both legacy and unified storage state\\n- `pkg/storage/legacysql/dualwrite/static.go` and `runtime.go` - Implement dual-write modes for simultaneous writes to both legacy and unified storage during migration\\n- `pkg/storage/legacysql/dualwrite/service.go` - Manages migration status and transitions\\n\\n## Migration Tables and Versioning\\n\\nAdditional migration files handle specific aspects:\\n- `pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/ualert/rule_group_index_migration.go` - Indexes for alert rule groups\\n- `pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/ualert/rule_creator_mig.go` - Tracks created_by and updated_by fields\\n- `pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/ualert/recording_rules_mig.go` - Support for Prometheus-style recording rules\\n- `pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/ualert/alert_rule_version_guid_mig.go` - GUID tracking for alert rules across versions\\n- `pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/ualert/rule_notification_settings_mig.go` - Notification settings columns\\n- `pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/ualert/created_folders_mig.go` - Folder creation tracking during migration\\n\\n## Configuration Management\\n\\n- `pkg/setting/setting_unified_alerting.go` - Handles configuration for unified alerting, including settings fallback from legacy to unified alerting configuration\\n- `pkg/services/provisioning/provisioning.go` - Main provisioning service that manages alert provisioning\\n- `pkg/services/provisioning/alerting/rules_provisioner.go` - Implements `AlertRuleProvisioner` interface\\n\\nThe migration uses a dual-write pattern where both legacy and unified storage systems are written to during the transition period, with configurable read preferences. The system tracks migration status per organization in a key-value store, allowing for granular control of the migration process.\"\n}\n",
